    TVPSPORTV5-1237
    Initial check in caused an unstable build. Investigations led to the following changes:
    - copyOnRead set on sitemap cache to ensure immutability
    - increased cache size which will ensure that test option sitemaps will be cached alongside each other, and thus create scenarios more in keeping with LIVE
    - @SharedExecution reinstated, despite known potential issues with serving up the wrong version of a sitemap  on environments up to and including TEST when there is large load and the cache has expired.
    Reviewed by Matt Mould and Graeme Phillipson.
